if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '66ced46a69f468f549475e3b88579dec0cbcb392') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '66ced46a69f468f549475e3b88579dec0cbcb392') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '72a66559e1267a6357cd72aedb17ffd3b1e1bdde') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '66ced46a69f468f549475e3b88579dec0cbcb392') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != '150f6913aa9f692fe40c34caf7b9d23f24e940b4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '150f6913aa9f692fe40c34caf7b9d23f24e940b4') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '69d1654c93455255727fd267b9c837707a5e0653') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '150f6913aa9f692fe40c34caf7b9d23f24e940b4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php') != '656cf4d5f326ff8b343b1d961a7f025cc5bbc4a0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php') !== '656cf4d5f326ff8b343b1d961a7f025cc5bbc4a0') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php') !== '59f78fbe763617ed8a68aade74a93a63b0f78d2f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php') !== '656cf4d5f326ff8b343b1d961a7f025cc5bbc4a0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/db_updates/update1001.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '01f4702f76dcfb7991a830404f17f564d467f4e6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '01f4702f76dcfb7991a830404f17f564d467f4e6') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '12b2b2ef101bdabd132daaae8a0cf1825c58f242') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '01f4702f76dcfb7991a830404f17f564d467f4e6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/database/pdo/OIDplusDatabasePluginPDOSetup.js') !== 'c4e7f6ea717e92d9bc9a93ed0244849c4acba617') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/database/pdo/OIDplusDatabasePluginPDOSetup.js');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1231\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1231') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
